He offered Ruben on a bagel.... Okay, so I ask, Can I get a discount of you're going to serve me a Ruben on a bagel, because I feel like it would be degrading to the Ruben to do so. Used to be a 4 star review but updating today.  I just experienced one of the most outrageous examples of unprofessional behavior by a "manager" of a retail store.   I went into Petsmart today to buy crickets.  When I walked in the person who stands there greeting people said hello and if I needed anything.  I was talking to someone on the phone and I indicated I was OK. at that moment.  Eventually I would need crickets but I had other shopping to do first.   When I returned to the area where the Crickets were I stood there for quite some time. Other people were also walking up and down the aisles looking for assistance and one person had to go up to the registers to get someone to come back and help him near the turtle supplies.  I stood there for over 10 minutes and not one person showed up or check the area at all. I was not the only person waiting for assistance.

I got disgusted and decided to leave the store.  I have been shopping at this store for years.  As I was leaving the "manager" who I didn't know was the manager was near the entrance with other employees and I overheard him giving some direction to the employees.  I commented to him as I walked by without stopping, "maybe you should have someone come back and check on people standing around for over 10 minutes waiting to buy crickets"

I was walking at a brisk pace because now I had to drive another 7 miles to find somewhere that would be able to sell me crickets.   The manager came literally running out of the store to argue with me stating that "we tried to help you and when you came in you said you didn't need help".   I then told him that I didn't need help as I was walking through the doors and that doesn't excuse standing in a location for 10 minutes and being ignored.  For clarity I talk loudly as a baseline.  I am a veteran, and I have a fairly significant hearing loss so I tend to talk loud.  As I'm walking to my car this "manager" "Juan" continues to argue with me telling me that I'm yelling.  Which is irrelevant because I can yell all I want.  I'm outside walking to my car. There are no laws stating I can't yell.  I then turned around to him and stated that he hasn't heard me yell and than put on foghorn blast to make a point.   I was born and raised in New Jersey and worked with Adolescents for nearly 15 years.  I can be loud if necessary.

"Juan" continues to follow me to my car, literally trying to antagonize me and when I gave him a demonstration of yelling to provide clarity that my normal tone of voice is far from yelling he then starts telling me that he is calling the police and follows me to my car and starts taking pictures of my license plate.   I told him he can call anyone he wants.  There are no laws on the books that say I can't yell at "Juan".  This is part of the California entitled snowflake mentality.   Someone needs to put his big boy pants on and grow up.  I actually hope that he did call the police because his actions to which I have a witness were clearly intentional and  antagonistic. For him to follow me out of the store trying to create a conflict is outrageous.

As long as Petsmart employes him I will no longer be a customer. There are too many other places where I can shop to put up with childish unprofessional antics of a bruised ego of an incompetent manager.   In fact when I called the store from the parking lot before I left asking for the name of the manager it wasn't him at all.  He is not the manager.  He is the assistant manager.  I will absolutely be taking this to their corporate office on Monday.   I've dealt with a lot of nonsense from insurance companies and other organizations that think they have you over the barrel  I have never been confronted with a "manager" who conducted himself in such an unprofessional manner.

Juan is going to learn a lesson about conducting himself appropriately because I am going to make sure that this is broadcast from end of the planet to another.< /Text>
